in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;

out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;

out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;

out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
float u_xlat9;
float u_xlat21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat9 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_16;
mediump float u_xlat16_18;
mediump float u_xlat16_30;
float u_xlat36;
bool u_xlatb36;
float u_xlat38;
bool u_xlatb39;
mediump float u_xlat16_40;
mediump float u_xlat16_41;
mediump float u_xlat16_44;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.x + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb36 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb36 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb36){discard;}
    u_xlat16_1.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_1.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = max(u_xlat36, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat36) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_1.w + _MetallicOffset;

void main()
{

    u_xlatb36 = u_xlat16_1<0.0;
    if(u_xlatb36){discard;}
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    u_xlat36 = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat2.xy).x;
    u_xlatb36 = u_xlat36<u_xlat2.z;
    u_xlat1.x = (u_xlatb36) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    u_xlat36 = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat2.xy).x;
    u_xlatb36 = u_xlat36<u_xlat2.z;
    u_xlat1.y = (u_xlatb36) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    u_xlat36 = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat2.xy).x;
    u_xlatb36 = u_xlat36<u_xlat2.z;

    u_xlatb2 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
    u_xlatb36 = u_xlatb36 || u_xlatb2;

    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);

    u_xlat2.x = exp2(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + _ShadowOffset;
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_5.xyz = max(u_xlat16_5.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));

    u_xlat16_17.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * u_xlat16_17.xyz;
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = max(u_xlat16_17.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));

	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _RimLightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _faceshadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _FresnelColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _FresnelFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainPlayerPositionWS;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _RampMap_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MatColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MatMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHColorScale;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
float u_xlat9;
float u_xlat21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat9 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
bool u_xlatb2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
vec4 u_xlat6;
mediump float u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_7;
bool u_xlatb7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
vec3 u_xlat14;
float u_xlat15;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_16;
mediump float u_xlat16_18;
bool u_xlatb19;
mediump float u_xlat16_30;
float u_xlat38;
mediump float u_xlat16_40;
mediump float u_xlat16_41;
mediump float u_xlat16_44;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyw = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).yzx;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat16_1.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_1.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat14.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_1.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot((-u_xlat14.xyz), u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x + u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * (-u_xlat16_5.xxx) + (-u_xlat14.xyz);
    u_xlat16_41 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat14.xyz);
    u_xlat16_41 = abs(u_xlat16_41) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_41 = min(u_xlat16_41, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_6 = u_xlat16_1.w * u_xlat16_1.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_6 = max(u_xlat16_6, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_6 = min(u_xlat16_6, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_18 = (-u_xlat16_6) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_18 = u_xlat16_18 * u_xlat16_6;
    u_xlat16_18 = u_xlat16_18 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_2 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_18);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_2.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_18 = u_xlat16_6 * u_xlat16_6;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_18 * u_xlat16_18 + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].xxx + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].zzz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[3].xyz * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].www + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat38 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat38 = u_xlat38 + vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat38 = u_xlat38 * 0.5;
    u_xlat7.x = u_xlat38 * _RampMap_ST.x + _RampMap_ST.z;
    u_xlat7.y = 0.0;
    u_xlat16_7 = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat7.xy);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_7.w;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * _MatColor.xyz + (-u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xxx * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_40;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_30 = min(max(u_xlat16_30, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_30 = clamp(u_xlat16_30, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_40 = (-u_xlat16_40) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_40 = (-u_xlat16_40) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_40 = (-u_xlat16_6) + u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_40 = min(max(u_xlat16_40, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_40 = clamp(u_xlat16_40, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_30) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_5.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_30) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat38 = (-u_xlat16_41) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_40 = (-u_xlat16_41) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat38 * u_xlat38;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * u_xlat16_41;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_41) * u_xlat9.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat38 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat38 = inversesqrt(u_xlat38);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat38) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat38 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat38 = min(max(u_xlat38, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat38 = clamp(u_xlat38, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.x = (-u_xlat38) * u_xlat38 + 1.0;
    u_xlat38 = u_xlat16_18 * u_xlat38;
    u_xlat38 = u_xlat38 * u_xlat38 + u_xlat3.x;
    u_xlat38 = u_xlat16_18 / u_xlat38;
    u_xlat38 = u_xlat38 * u_xlat38;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat16_6 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat15 = u_xlat16_6 + 1.0;
    u_xlat15 = u_xlat15 * u_xlat15;
    u_xlat38 = u_xlat38 * u_xlat3.x;
    u_xlat38 = min(u_xlat38, 100.0);
    u_xlat3.xzw = vec3(u_xlat38) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat38 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat38 = min(max(u_xlat38, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat38 = clamp(u_xlat38, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.xzw = vec3(u_xlat38) * u_xlat3.xzw;
    u_xlat38 = log2(u_xlat38);

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
vec4 u_xlat6;
mediump float u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_16;
mediump float u_xlat16_18;
mediump float u_xlat16_30;
float u_xlat36;
bool u_xlatb36;
float u_xlat38;
bool u_xlatb39;
mediump float u_xlat16_40;
mediump float u_xlat16_41;
mediump float u_xlat16_44;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.x + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb36 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb36 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb36){discard;}
    u_xlat16_1.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_1.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = max(u_xlat36, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat36) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_1.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot((-u_xlat2.xyz), u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x + u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * (-u_xlat16_5.xxx) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_41 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_41 = abs(u_xlat16_41) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_41 = min(u_xlat16_41, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_6 = u_xlat16_1.w * u_xlat16_1.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_6 = max(u_xlat16_6, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_6 = min(u_xlat16_6, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_18 = (-u_xlat16_6) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_18 = u_xlat16_18 * u_xlat16_6;
    u_xlat16_18 = u_xlat16_18 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_2 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_18);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_2.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_18 = u_xlat16_6 * u_xlat16_6;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat16_18 * u_xlat16_18 + 1.0;
    u_xlat36 = float(1.0) / u_xlat36;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].xxx + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].zzz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[3].xyz * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].www + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat36 + vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat36 * 0.5;
    u_xlat7.x = u_xlat36 * _RampMap_ST.x + _RampMap_ST.z;
    u_xlat7.y = 0.0;
    u_xlat16_7 = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat7.xy);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_0.y * u_xlat16_7.w;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * _MatColor.xyz + (-u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xxx * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_40;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_30 = min(max(u_xlat16_30, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_30 = clamp(u_xlat16_30, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_40 = (-u_xlat16_40) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_40 = (-u_xlat16_40) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_40 = (-u_xlat16_6) + u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_40 = min(max(u_xlat16_40, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_40 = clamp(u_xlat16_40, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_30) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_5.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_30) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat12 = (-u_xlat16_41) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_40 = (-u_xlat16_41) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat12 * u_xlat12;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * u_xlat16_41;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_41) * u_xlat9.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat12 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat12 = inversesqrt(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat12 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat12 = min(max(u_xlat12, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat12 = clamp(u_xlat12, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat36 = (-u_xlat12) * u_xlat12 + 1.0;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat16_18 * u_xlat12;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat12 * u_xlat12 + u_xlat36;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat16_18 / u_xlat12;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat12 * u_xlat12;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat16_6 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat38 = u_xlat16_6 + 1.0;
    u_xlat38 = u_xlat38 * u_xlat38;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat12 * u_xlat36;
    u_xlat12 = min(u_xlat12, 100.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat12 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat12 = min(max(u_xlat12, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat12 = clamp(u_xlat12, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat12 = log2(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat12 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat12 = exp2(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat12 + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat12 = min(max(u_xlat12, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat12 = clamp(u_xlat12, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_41 = dot(u_xlat6, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_44 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_44;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb36 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb36 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb39 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb39 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb36 = u_xlatb36 || u_xlatb39;
    u_xlat16_41 = (u_xlatb36) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_41;
    u_xlat7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_41) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = min(u_xlat16_10.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = max(u_xlat16_10.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = max(u_xlat16_10.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_44 = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_44 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_44);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_44) * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_44 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_10.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_44 = min(max(u_xlat16_44, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_44 = clamp(u_xlat16_44, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD8.yyy * _AddlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_44) * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = max(u_xlat16_10.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = min(u_xlat16_10.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat38 * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_44 = (-u_xlat38) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_44 + u_xlat12;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 / u_xlat16_44;
    u_xlat16_44 = dot(_RimLightDir.xyz, _RimLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_44 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_44);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_44) * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_10.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_4.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_16.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_16.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_16.x;

    u_xlat16_5.x = (-u_xlat16_42) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat12 * u_xlat12;
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_17.x * u_xlat16_17.x;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 + (-u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat16_41 + 1.0;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat12 * u_xlat12;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_40 = clamp(u_xlat16_40, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat11.xyz = (-u_xlat7.xyz) + vec3(u_xlat16_40);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_17.xxx * u_xlat11.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * u_xlat10.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_40 = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_40 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_40);
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_40 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_17.xyz);
    u_xlat16_40 = clamp(u_xlat16_40, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD8.yyy * _AddlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) * u_xlat16_17.xyz;
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * u_xlat16_17.xyz;
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = max(u_xlat16_17.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = min(u_xlat16_17.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz + u_xlat16_17.xyz;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat12 * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_40 = (-u_xlat12) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat16_40 + u_xlat36;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_5.x / u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(_RimLightDir.xyz, _RimLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_4.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_16 = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_16 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_16;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_16 * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat16_4.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_16;
    u_xlat16_16 = (-_RimlightShadowScale) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_16 + _RimlightShadowScale;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat16_6.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = max(u_xlat16_4.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = min(u_xlat16_4.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat10_0.z * _Emissive;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_0.x;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 * _EmisssionScale;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_39) * u_xlat10_2.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    return;
}

in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;

out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;

mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
float u_xlat9;
float u_xlat21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat9 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightData;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightIndices[2];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_ProbesOcclusion;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(1) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _HairMap_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _BumpMapNr2_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SHScale;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHBotColor;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _specularColor2;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_2Y;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _faceshadowScale;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MatColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MatMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHColorScale;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat18;
float u_xlat19;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat8 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xzw = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * u_xlat1.xxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
float u_xlat11;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_15;
mediump float u_xlat16_17;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
float u_xlat33;
bool u_xlatb33;
float u_xlat35;
mediump float u_xlat16_37;
mediump float u_xlat16_38;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.x + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb33 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb33 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb33){discard;}
    u_xlat16_1.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_1.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat33 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = max(u_xlat33, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat33) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat33) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_1.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot((-u_xlat2.xyz), u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x + u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * (-u_xlat16_5.xxx) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = abs(u_xlat16_38) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_38 = min(u_xlat16_38, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_1.w * u_xlat16_1.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_6.x = max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(u_xlat16_6.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_17 * u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_17 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_2 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_17);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_2.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_6.x * u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat33 = u_xlat16_17 * u_xlat16_17 + 1.0;
    u_xlat33 = float(1.0) / u_xlat33;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].xxx + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].zzz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[3].xyz * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].www + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat33 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat33 = u_xlat33 + vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat33 = u_xlat33 * 0.5;
    u_xlat7.x = u_xlat33 * _RampMap_ST.x + _RampMap_ST.z;
    u_xlat7.y = 0.0;
    u_xlat16_7 = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat7.xy);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_0.y * u_xlat16_7.w;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * _MatColor.xyz + (-u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xxx * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_37;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_28 = min(max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_28 = clamp(u_xlat16_28, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_37) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_37) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) + u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_37 = min(max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_37 = clamp(u_xlat16_37, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_5.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_28) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat11 = (-u_xlat16_38) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_38) + 1.0;

    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_5.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_28) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat11 = (-u_xlat16_38) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_38) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat11 * u_xlat11;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat9.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat11 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat11 = inversesqrt(u_xlat11);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat11) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat11 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat11 = clamp(u_xlat11, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat33 = (-u_xlat11) * u_xlat11 + 1.0;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat16_17 * u_xlat11;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat11 * u_xlat11 + u_xlat33;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat16_17 / u_xlat11;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat11 * u_xlat11;
    u_xlat33 = u_xlat16_6.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat35 = u_xlat16_6.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat35 = u_xlat35 * u_xlat35;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat11 * u_xlat33;
    u_xlat11 = min(u_xlat11, 100.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat11) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat11 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat11 = clamp(u_xlat11, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat11) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat11 = log2(u_xlat11);
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat11 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat11 = exp2(u_xlat11);
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat11 + _ShadowOffset;
    u_xlat11 = clamp(u_xlat11, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = min(u_xlat16_6.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = max(u_xlat16_6.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat11) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = max(u_xlat16_6.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_38 = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_38);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_38 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = clamp(u_xlat16_38, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD8.yyy * _AddlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = max(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = min(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat35 * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat35) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_38 + u_xlat11;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 / u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat16_38 = dot(_RimLightDir.xyz, _RimLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_38);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_4.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_15.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_15.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_4.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = max(u_xlat16_4.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = min(u_xlat16_4.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat10_0.z * _Emissive;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_0.x;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * _EmisssionScale;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat10_1.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    return;
}

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat18;
float u_xlat19;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat8 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xzw = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * u_xlat1.xxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;

    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;

    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;

vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat18;
float u_xlat19;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat8 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xzw = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * u_xlat1.xxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
float u_xlat11;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_15;
mediump float u_xlat16_17;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
float u_xlat33;
bool u_xlatb33;
float u_xlat35;
mediump float u_xlat16_37;
mediump float u_xlat16_38;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.x + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb33 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb33 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb33){discard;}
    u_xlat16_1.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_1.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat33 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = max(u_xlat33, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat33) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat33) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_1.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot((-u_xlat2.xyz), u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x + u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * (-u_xlat16_5.xxx) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = abs(u_xlat16_38) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_38 = min(u_xlat16_38, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_1.w * u_xlat16_1.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_6.x = max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(u_xlat16_6.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_17 * u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_17 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_2 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_17);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_2.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_6.x * u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat33 = u_xlat16_17 * u_xlat16_17 + 1.0;
    u_xlat33 = float(1.0) / u_xlat33;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].xxx + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].zzz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[3].xyz * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixInvV[0].www + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat33 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat33 = u_xlat33 + vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat33 = u_xlat33 * 0.5;
    u_xlat7.x = u_xlat33 * _RampMap_ST.x + _RampMap_ST.z;
    u_xlat7.y = 0.0;
    u_xlat16_7 = texture(_RampMap, u_xlat7.xy);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_0.y * u_xlat16_7.w;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * _MatColor.xyz + (-u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xxx * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_37;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_28 = min(max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_28 = clamp(u_xlat16_28, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_37) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_37) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) + u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_37 = min(max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_37 = clamp(u_xlat16_37, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_5.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_28) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat11 = (-u_xlat16_38) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_38) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat11 * u_xlat11;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat9.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat11 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat11 = inversesqrt(u_xlat11);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat11) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat11 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat11 = min(max(u_xlat11, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat11 = clamp(u_xlat11, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat33 = (-u_xlat11) * u_xlat11 + 1.0;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat16_17 * u_xlat11;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat11 * u_xlat11 + u_xlat33;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat16_17 / u_xlat11;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat11 * u_xlat11;
    u_xlat33 = u_xlat16_6.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat35 = u_xlat16_6.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat35 = u_xlat35 * u_xlat35;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat11 * u_xlat33;
    u_xlat11 = min(u_xlat11, 100.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat11) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat11 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat11 = min(max(u_xlat11, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat11 = clamp(u_xlat11, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat11) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat11 = log2(u_xlat11);
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat11 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat11 = exp2(u_xlat11);
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat11 + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat11 = min(max(u_xlat11, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat11 = clamp(u_xlat11, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = min(u_xlat16_6.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = max(u_xlat16_6.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat11) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = max(u_xlat16_6.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_38 = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_38);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_38 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_8.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_38 = min(max(u_xlat16_38, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_38 = clamp(u_xlat16_38, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD8.yyy * _AddlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz;

#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat16_15.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_15.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_4.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_15.x;

    u_xlat16_4.xyz = max(u_xlat16_4.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = min(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat35 * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat35) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_38 + u_xlat11;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 / u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat16_38 = dot(_RimLightDir.xyz, _RimLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_38);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_4.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_15.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_15.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_4.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = max(u_xlat16_4.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = min(u_xlat16_4.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat10_0.z * _Emissive;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_0.x;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * _EmisssionScale;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat10_1.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    return;
}

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat8 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;

    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xzw = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat0.xzw;

    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * u_xlat1.xxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;

    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;

    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;

    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;

in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;

in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;

vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
bool u_xlatb2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;

float u_xlat14;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_15;
mediump float u_xlat16_17;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;

mediump float u_xlat16_37;
mediump float u_xlat16_38;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyw = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).yzx;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat16_1.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_1.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_1.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_1.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot((-u_xlat13.xyz), u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x + u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * (-u_xlat16_5.xxx) + (-u_xlat13.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat13.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = abs(u_xlat16_38) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_38 = min(u_xlat16_38, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_1.w * u_xlat16_1.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_6.x = max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(u_xlat16_6.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;

#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _OutlineMap;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec4 in_COLOR0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump float vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump float u_xlat16_3;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat12;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0 = 0.0;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_NORMAL0.zxy * in_TANGENT0.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_NORMAL0.yzx * in_TANGENT0.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * unity_WorldTransformParams.www;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_COLOR0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat1.yyy;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_TANGENT0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * u_xlat1.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat12 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat12 = max(u_xlat12, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat12 = inversesqrt(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat12 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat12 = inversesqrt(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat12 = dot(_lightDir.xyz, _lightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat12 = inversesqrt(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * _lightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat12 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat12 = min(max(u_xlat12, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat12 = clamp(u_xlat12, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-_OutlineColor.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat1.xyz + _OutlineColor.xyz;
    u_xlat2 = textureLod(_OutlineMap, in_TEXCOORD0.xy, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3 = max(u_xlat2.w, 0.200000003);
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat16_3 * 0.00999999978;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat0.yy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1].xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0].xy * u_xlat0.xx + u_xlat1.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2].xy * u_xlat0.zz + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat8 = dot(u_xlat0.xy, u_xlat0.xy);
    u_xlat8 = inversesqrt(u_xlat8);
    u_xlat0.xy = vec2(u_xlat8) * u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy / _ScreenParams.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * _ScreenResolution.yy;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat2 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat2;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * u_xlat1.ww;
    gl_Position.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(0.00462962966, 0.00462962966) + u_xlat1.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat12 / u_xlat1.w;
    gl_Position.z = u_xlat0.x + u_xlat1.z;
    gl_Position.w = u_xlat1.w;
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 300 es

precision highp float;
precision highp int;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
void main()
{
    SV_Target0.xyz = max(vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif
"
}
}
